    $(document).ready(function(){
        $("body").keypress(function(e){
            if (e.which == 110 ) {
                if ( !$("input, textarea, select").is(":focus") ) {
                    $("#hitroiskanje").focus();
                    var el = $("#hitroiskanje").get(0);
                    var elemLen = el.value.length;
                    el.selectionStart = elemLen;
                    el.selectionEnd = elemLen;
                    e.defaultPrevented();
                }
            }
        });
    });
        // /* AS: search suggestion */
        $(document).ready(function(){

            if ($( "#hitroiskanje" ).is(':visible'))
            {
                $(function() {
                    var cache = {},
                        lastXhr;
                    $( "#hitroiskanje" ).appendTo("#hitroiskanje").autocomplete({
                        minLength: 0,
                        source: function( request, response ) {
                            var term = request.term;

                            if ( term in cache ) {
                                response( cache[ term ] );
                                return;
                            }

                            lastXhr = $.getJSON( "/jq/facet-suggest.php", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {
                                cache[ term ] = data;

                                if ( xhr === lastXhr ) {
                                    response( data );
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
            else
            {
                $(function() {
                    var cache = {},
                        lastXhr;
                    $( "#m-hitroiskanje" ).appendTo("#m-hitroiskanje").autocomplete({
                        minLength: 0,
                        source: function( request, response ) {
                            var term = request.term;

                            if ( term in cache ) {
                                response( cache[ term ] );
                                return;
                            }

                            lastXhr = $.getJSON( "/jq/facet-suggest.php", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {
                                cache[ term ] = data;

                                if ( xhr === lastXhr ) {
                                    response( data );
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
        });

        jQuery(function($) {
            $("a.fav").click(function(e){
                e.defaultPrevented(); // this will prevent the anchor tag from going the user off to the link
                var bookmarkUrl = this.href;
                var bookmarkTitle = 'Stanovanje Oddaja J. Primorska | NEPREMICNINE.net';
                if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('chrome') > -1) {
                    alert("This function is not available in Google Chrome. Click the star symbol at the end of the address-bar or hit Ctrl-D (Command+D for Macs) to create a bookmark.");
                } else if (window.sidebar) { // For Mozilla Firefox Bookmark
                    window.sidebar.addPanel(bookmarkTitle, bookmarkUrl,"");
                } else if( window.external || document.all) { // For IE Favorite
                    window.external.AddFavorite( bookmarkUrl, bookmarkTitle);
                } else if(window.opera) { // For Opera Browsers
                    $("a.bookmark").attr("href",bookmarkUrl);
                    $("a.bookmark").attr("title",bookmarkTitle);
                    $("a.bookmark").attr("rel","sidebar");
                } else { // for other browsers which does not support
                    alert('Your browser does not support this bookmark action');
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });

        $(document).ready (function () {
            $('.jq-confirm').click (function () {
                var title = 'Želite opraviti akcijo';

                if ($(this).attr("title").length > 0)
                    title = $(this).attr("title");
                else if ($(this).data('bs-original-title').length > 0)
                    title = $(this).data('bs-original-title');

                return confirm (title + "?") ;
            }) ;

            $('.jq-confirm-delete').click (function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var url = $(this).attr('href');
                if (confirm ($(this).attr ("title")))
                {

                    var ogl_cnt = parseInt($('.ogl-num').html());
                    $('.ogl-num').each(function( index ) {
                        $(this).text(ogl_cnt -1);
                    });

                    if ($(this).data("active") == 't')
                        $('#vpis-stat td.cnt_ogl_t').html(parseInt($('#vpis-stat td.cnt_ogl_t').html() - 1));
                    else
                        $('#vpis-stat td.cnt_ogl_f').html(parseInt($('#vpis-stat td.cnt_ogl_f').html() - 1));

                    $.get( url, function( data ) {
                        //$( ".result" ).html( data );
                    });
                    $(this).closest('.oglas').slideUp('slow', function()
                    {
                        alert('Oglas je bil uspešno izbrisan.');
                    });

                }
            });

	        $('.jq-confirm-deakt').click (function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var url = $(this).attr('href');
                if (confirm ($(this).attr ("title")))
                {

                    var ogl_cnt = parseInt($('.ogl-num').html());
                    $('.ogl-num').each(function( index ) {
                        $(this).text(ogl_cnt -1);
                    });

                    $.get( url, function( data ) {
                        //$( ".result" ).html( data );
                    });
                    $(this).closest('.oglas').slideUp('slow', function()
                    {
                        alert('Oglas je bil uspešno deaktiviran.');
                    });

                }
            }) ;

            $('body').on('click', 'a.jq-confirm-24h', function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                var url = $(this).attr('href');
                if (confirm ($(this).attr ("title")))
                {
                    var btn = $(this);

                    $.get( url, function( data ) {
                        var count = (data.match(/24h-OK/g) || []).length;
                        if (count == 2) {
                            btn.attr("href", "javascript:void();");
                            btn.removeClass('jq-confirm-24h');
                            btn.css('color','#777');
                            btn.attr('title', 'Ponovna objava oglasa v rubriki 24 ur je možna po enem mesecu');

                            //change 24h count
                            var cnt_24h = parseInt($('#cnt_24h').html());
                            $('#cnt_24h').text(cnt_24h + 1);

                            alert('Oglas je bil uspešno objavljen v rubriki 24 ur.');
                        }
                        else
                            alert('Oglas ni bil ponovno objavljen v rubriki 24 ur.');
                    });
                }
            }) ;




        }) ;

    jQuery(function($) {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $("a.btn-slide").mouseover(function() {
                $("#top-panel").stop(true, true).slideDown("fast");
                $(this).addClass("active");
            });
            $("#moje-nep").mouseleave(function() {
                if ( !$('#moje-nep input[type=text]').is(":focus") ) {
                    $("#top-panel").delay(1000).slideUp("slow");
                    $(this).removeClass("active");
                }
            });
        });
        $(".flogin").bind("keyup change", function () {
          $(this).val(function(i, v) { return v.replace(/  /g," "); });
        });

        $(document).bind('click', function(e) {
            if( $(e.target).closest('#moje-nep').length === 0 ) {
                $("#top-panel").delay(1000).slideUp("slow");
            }
        });
    });

    
        jQuery(function($) {
            $(document).ready(function() {
                $("#fqrun").click(function() {
                    $("li.iskalnik").addClass("open");
                     $("#header").css('z-index', 500);
                    $(".iskalnik ul").stop(true, true).slideDown("fast");
                });
                $("li.iskalnik").mouseover(function() {
                     $("#header").css('z-index', 500);
                    $(".iskalnik ul").stop(true, true).slideDown("fast");
                    $(this).addClass("open");
                });
                $("li.iskalnik").mouseleave(function() {
                    if ($('.iskalnik input[type=text]').is(":focus")) {
                        $('input[type=text]').focus(function(){
                            $(this).css({'background-color' : '#FCC'});
                        });
                        $('input[type=text]').blur(function(){
                            $(this).css({'background-color' : '#fff'});
                        });
                    } else {
                        if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry/i.test(navigator.userAgent) == false ) {
                            $(".iskalnik ul").delay(500).slideUp("slow", function(){
                                 $("#header").css('z-index', 300);
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    $(".iskalnik select").mouseleave(function(event){
                        event.stopPropagation();
                    });
                    //$(this).removeClass("open");
                });

                $(document).bind('click', function(e) {
                    if( $(e.target).closest('li.iskalnik.open').length === 0 && $(e.target).closest('#moje-nep').length === 0 ) {
                        $("li.iskalnik.open ul").delay(500).slideUp("slow", function(){
                            $("#header").css('z-index', 300);
                        });
                        $("#top-panel").delay(1000).slideUp("slow");
                  }
                });

            });
        });
    


    function rSel (r) {
        $.post("/jq/r-sel.php", {id:r,rsel:'2'}, function(data) {
            $("select#NOr").html(data);
            $("select#NOr").removeAttr("disabled");
        }).done(function(){serialize_search();});
    }

    $(function(){
        $('input:radio[name=d]').change(function() {
            $("select#NOr").attr("disabled","disabled");
            $("select#NOr").html("<option>nalagam...</option>");

            $("select#NOue1").attr("disabled","disabled");
            $("select#NOue1").html("<option>nalagam...</option>");

            var id = $(this).val();

            $.post("/jq/r-sel.php", {id:id,rsel:'2'}, function(data) {
                $("select#NOr").html(data);
                $("select#NOr").removeAttr("disabled");
            }).done(function(){
                /*mobile only*/
                if ($('.NOue').is(':visible')) {
                    var id = $("select#NOr").val();
                    $.post("/jq/ue-sel.php", {id:id, input:'select'}, function(data) {
                        $("select#NOue1").html(data);
                        $("select#NOue1").removeAttr("disabled");
                    }).done(function(){serialize_search();});
                }
                else {
                    var select = $('#NOr>option');
                    select[0].selected = true;
        			serialize_search();
                }
            });
            //$('#NOr')[0].selectedIndex = 0;
            /*var select = $('#NOr>option');
            select[0].selected = true;
			serialize_search();*/
        });


        $('select#NOr').change(function() {
            var id = $(this).val();

            $("select#NOue1").attr("disabled","disabled");
            $("select#NOue1").html("<option>nalagam...</option>");

            $.post("/jq/ue-sel.php", {id:id, input:'select'}, function(data) {
                $("select#NOue1").html(data);
                $("select#NOue1").removeAttr("disabled");
            }).done(function(){serialize_search();});
        });

    });

    $(document).ready(function()
    {
        $("input:text").focus(function()
        {
            if ($(this).val() == $(this)[0].title)
            {
                $(this).removeClass("grey");
                $(this).val("");
            }
        });

        $("input:text").blur(function()
        {
            if ($(this).val() == "")
            {
                $(this).addClass("grey");
                $(this).val($(this)[0].title);
            }
        });

        $("input:text").blur();
    });

<script type="text/javascript">

// Preloader
$(window).on('load resize', function() {
    $('#preloader').fadeOut(0);
    $('body').css({'overflow':'visible'});
})

window.middle_h_screen = (screen.width/2)-300;
window.middle_v_screen = (screen.height/2)-175;

function popupCenter(url, title, w, h) {
    // Fixes dual-screen position Most browsers Firefox
    var dualScreenLeft = window.screenLeft != undefined ? window.screenLeft : screen.left;
    var dualScreenTop = window.screenTop != undefined ? window.screenTop : screen.top;
    width = window.innerWidth ? window.innerWidth : document.documentElement.clientWidth ? document.documentElement.clientWidth : screen.width;
    height = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : document.documentElement.clientHeight ? document.documentElement.clientHeight : screen.height;

    var left = ((width / 2) - (w / 2)) + dualScreenLeft;
    var top = ((height / 2) - (h / 2)) + dualScreenTop;
    var newWindow = window.open(url, title, 'scrollbars=yes, width=' + w + ', height=' + h + ', top=' + top + ', left=' + left);

    // Puts focus on the newWindow
    if (window.focus) {
    newWindow.focus();
    }
}

// generate notes
function generate(type, text, id) {

            var n = noty({
                text        : text,
                type        : type,
                dismissQueue: true,
                layout      : 'bottomLeft',
                closeWith   : ['button'],
                theme       : 'relax',
                maxVisible  : 5,
                animation   : {
                    open  : 'animated bounceInLeft',
                    close : 'animated bounceOutLeft',
                    easing: 'swing',
                    speed : 500
                },
                callback: {
                    onClose: function() {
                        $.ajax({ url: '/jq/set_noted.php?id=' + id });
                    }
                }
            });
            //console.log('html: ' + n.options.id);
        }

        function generateAll() {
                        //generate('success');
        }

        $(document).ready(function () {

            setTimeout(function() {
                generateAll();
            }, 500);

            setInterval(function() {
                var exclude = '?';
                $( ".notification-identifier" ).each(function( index ) {
                    //console.log( index + ": " + $( this ).text() );
                    exclude += 'exclude[]=' + $( this ).text() + '&';
                });
                $.get( "/jq/check_notifications.php" + exclude, function( data ) {
                    $( "body" ).append( data );
                });
            }, 1000 * 1000 * 1); // refresh every 10 minutes


            var popup = false;
            if (mobileAndTabletcheck() && $('#logo-m').is(':visible'))
              popup = true;
            $('#notification-bell a').webuiPopover({title:'<i class="fa fa-bell"></i> &nbsp; Obvestila',content:'Content',width:250,height:200,placement:'bottom-left',type:'async',url:'/jq/popover_notifications.php',cache:false,closeable:true,backdrop:popup});
            $('#notification-message a').webuiPopover({title:'<i class="fa fa-envelope"></i> &nbsp; Sporočila',content:'Content',width:250,height:200,placement:'bottom-left',type:'async',url:'/jq/popover_messages.php',cache:false,closeable:true,backdrop:popup});

            /*Search popup*/
            $('.burger-nav-search > a').on('click', function () {
                $(".mobile-search").dialog({
                    modal: true,
                    title: 'Iskalnik',
                    resizable: false,
                    dialogClass: 'mobile-search-dialog',
                    open: function( event, ui ) {
                        var id = $('select#NOr').val();
                        $.post("/jq/ue-sel.php", {id:id, input:'select'}, function(data) {
                            $("select#NOue1").html(data);
                        }).done(function(){serialize_search();});
                    },
                    buttons: {
                        'Confirm': {
                                click: function () {
                                    $('.ui-dialog .gumb.potrdi')[0].click();

                                },
                                text: 'Prikaži rezultate',
                                class: 'ui-ok'
                            },
                        "Cancel": {
                                click: function () {
                                    $(this).dialog("destroy");
                                },
                                text: 'Zapri',
                                class: 'ui-cancle'
                            }
                      }
                });
            });

            // messaging
            $(".inquiry-form").submit(function(event){
                event.preventDefault();
                event.stopPropagation();
                var id = $(this).find("#ad_id").val();
                var owner = $(this).find("#owner").val();
                var conversation = $(this).find("#conversation").val();
                var message = $(this).find("textarea").val();
                if (id && message){
                    $.post( "/jq/message_send.php", { id: id, owner: owner, message: message, conversation: conversation }, function(data){
                        //console.log(data.answer);
                        if (data.answer == 'success')
                        {
                            var last_message = data.last_message;
                            if ($("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list li").length){
                                $("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list li[key='" + (last_message*1 - 1) + "']").after('<li class="me" key="' + last_message + '"><img src="' + data.image + '" /><h4>' + data.username + '<br /><small> poslano ' + data.time + '</small></h4>' + data.message + '</li>');
                            } else {
                                $("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list").append('<li class="me" key="' + last_message + '"><img src="' + data.image + '" /><h4>' + data.username + '<br /><small> poslano ' + data.time + '</small></h4>' + data.message + '</li>');
                            }
                            $(".inquiry-form textarea").val('');
                            $("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list").perfectScrollbar('update');
                            $("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list").animate({ scrollTop: $("#conversation-" + conversation + " .messages-list")[0].scrollHeight}, 1000);
                        }
                    } );
                }
                //event.preventDefault();
            });

            // check for messages
            
            // initialise scrollbar
            if ($(".messages-list").length){
                $(".messages-list").perfectScrollbar();
                $('.messages-list').scrollTop($('.messages-list')[0].scrollHeight); // scroll to the bottom
            }

            if ($(".sender-info").length){
                $(".sender-info").each(function(index){
                    var conversation_id = $(this).attr("conversation");
                    var ad_id = $(this).attr("ad_id");
                    var owner = $("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " #owner").val();
                    $(this).click(function(){
                        $(this).parent().addClass('shown');
                        $(".conversation-container").not("#conversation-" + conversation_id).slideUp("fast");
                        $(".conversation-ad-info").not("#conversation-info-" + conversation_id).slideUp("fast");

                        if ($("#conversation-" + conversation_id).is(":visible"))
                        {
                            $("#conversation-" + conversation_id).slideUp('fast');
                            $("#conversation-info-" + conversation_id).slideUp('fast');
                        }
                        else
                        {

                            $("#conversation-" + conversation_id).slideDown("fast", function(){
                                $("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " .messages-list").scrollTop($("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " .messages-list")[0].scrollHeight); // scroll to the bottom
                            });
                            $("#conversation-info-" + conversation_id).slideDown("fast");
                        }
                        $(this).removeClass("unread");
                        $(this).parent().removeClass("unread");
                        $.post( "/jq/message_update.php", { id: ad_id, owner: owner, conversation: conversation_id, update_change: 'read' }, function(data){
                            //console.log(data.answer);
                            if (data.answer == 'success')
                            {
                                if (data.message_count)
                                {
                                    if ($("#notification-message a").find('span').length)
                                    {
                                        $("#notification-message a").find('span').text(data.message_count);
                                    } else {
                                        $("#notification-message a").append('<span>' + data.message_count + '</span>');
                                    }
                                    $("#notification-message a").addClass('active');

                                    $(".html-msg-count").text('(' + data.message_count + ')');
                                } else {
                                    $("#notification-message a").find('span').remove();
                                    $("#notification-message a").removeClass('active');

                                    $(".html-msg-count").text('');
                                }
                            }
                        } );

                    });
                });
            }

            // get message hash values
            var hash_value = window.location.hash.substr(1);
            if (hash_value){
                //alert(hash_value);
                if (hash_value.indexOf(":") > -1)
                {
                    var split_value = hash_value.split(":")
                    var action_value = split_value[0];
                    var m_value = split_value[1];
                } else {
                    if(hash_value.match(/^[0-9]+$/) != null)
                    {
                        //alert(hash_value);
                        $([document.documentElement, document.body]).animate({
                            scrollTop: $("#o-" + hash_value).offset().top -20
                        }, 1000);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        var action_value = hash_value;
                        var m_value = 0;
                    }
                }


                window.messages_updated = false;

                if (action_value == 'scroll_messages' && !m_value){
                    $('html, body').animate({
                        scrollTop: $("#get-info").offset().top
                    }, 1000, 'swing', function(){
                        if (!window.messages_updated)
                        {
                            window.messages_updated = true;
                            var ad_id = $("#ad_id").val();
                            var owner = $("#owner").val();
                            var conversation_id = $("#conversation").val();

                            $.post( "/jq/message_update.php", { id: ad_id, owner: owner, conversation: conversation_id, update_change: 'read' }, function(data){
                                if (data.answer == 'success')
                                {

                                    if (data.message_count)
                                    {
                                        if ($("#notification-message a").find('span').length)
                                        {
                                            $("#notification-message a").find('span').text(data.message_count);
                                        } else {
                                            $("#notification-message a").append('<span>' + data.message_count + '</span>');
                                        }
                                        $("#notification-message a").addClass('active');

                                        $(".html-msg-count").text('(' + data.message_count + ')');
                                    } else {
                                        $("#notification-message a").find('span').remove();
                                        $("#notification-message a").removeClass('active');

                                        $(".html-msg-count").text('');
                                    }
                                }

                            } );
                        }
                    });
                }

                if (action_value == 'scroll_messages' && m_value){
                    var conversation_id = m_value;
                    $("#sender-conversation-" + m_value).parent().addClass('shown');
                    $('html, body').animate({
                        scrollTop: $("#sender-conversation-" + m_value).offset().top
                    }, 1000, 'swing', function(){
                        $(".conversation-container").not("#conversation-" + conversation_id).slideUp("fast");
                        $(".conversation-ad-info").not("#conversation-info-" + conversation_id).slideUp("fast");
                        $("#conversation-" + conversation_id).slideDown("fast", function(){
                            $("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " .messages-list").scrollTop($("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " .messages-list")[0].scrollHeight); // scroll to the bottom
                            $("#sender-conversation-" + conversation_id).removeClass("unread");
                            $("#sender-conversation-" + conversation_id).parent().removeClass("unread");
                            var ad_id = $("#sender-conversation-" + conversation_id).attr('ad_id');
                            var owner = $("#conversation-" + conversation_id + " #owner").val();

                            if (!window.messages_updated)
                            {
                                window.messages_updated = true;
                                $.post( "/jq/message_update.php", { id: ad_id, owner: owner, conversation: conversation_id, update_change: 'read' }, function(data){
                                    //console.log(data.answer);
                                    if (data.answer == 'success')
                                    {
                                        //alert('yay');
                                        if (data.message_count)
                                        {
                                            if ($("#notification-message a").find('span').length)
                                            {
                                                $("#notification-message a").find('span').text(data.message_count);
                                            } else {
                                                $("#notification-message a").append('<span>' + data.message_count + '</span>');
                                            }
                                            $("#notification-message a").addClass('active');

                                            $(".html-msg-count").text('(' + data.message_count + ')');
                                        } else {
                                            $("#notification-message a").find('span').remove();
                                            $("#notification-message a").removeClass('active');

                                            $(".html-msg-count").text('');
                                        }
                                    }

                                } );
                            }
                        });
                        $("#conversation-info-" + conversation_id).slideDown("fast");
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        function update_read(element){
            var ad_id = $(element).parent().find("#ad_id").val();
            var owner = $(element).parent().find("#owner").val();
            var conversation_id = $(element).parent().find("#conversation").val();
            $.post( "/jq/message_update.php", { id: ad_id, owner: owner, conversation: conversation_id, update_change: 'read' }, function(data){
                if (data.answer == 'success')
                {
                    if (data.message_count)
                    {
                        if ($("#notification-message a").find('span').length)
                        {
                            $("#notification-message a").find('span').text(data.message_count);
                        } else {
                            $("#notification-message a").append('<span>' + data.message_count + '</span>');
                        }
                        $("#notification-message a").addClass('active');

                        $(".html-msg-count").text('(' + data.message_count + ')');
                    } else {
                        $("#notification-message a").find('span').remove();
                        $("#notification-message a").removeClass('active');

                        $(".html-msg-count").text('');
                    }
                }
            } );
        }

        function txt_auto_grow(element) {
            element.style.height = "5px";
            element.style.height = (element.scrollHeight)+"px";
        }

            var $dropdown = $('div.dropdownWrapper'),
              $drpBtn   = $dropdown.find('div.dropdownLabel');

        // search form
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            $("#NOsearch input").keyup(function(){
                serialize_search();
            });
            $("#NOsearch input[type='radio'], #NOsearch select").change(function(){
                serialize_search();
            });

            if ($("#naselja-izbira.scroll").length){
                $("#naselja-izbira").perfectScrollbar();
            }
        });

        function serialize_search()
        {
            if (mobileAndTabletcheck() && $('#logo-m').is(':visible') && $(".mobile-search #NOsearch").length > 0)
              var s_data = $(".mobile-search #NOsearch").serialize();
            else
              var s_data = $("#NOsearch").serialize();

            $.post( "/jq/search.php?wpg=nepremicnine&" + s_data, function( data ) {
              $("#NOsearch a.gumb.potrdi").attr('href', data);
            });
        }

        function block_user(conversation_id, username)
        {
            var r = confirm("Želite blokirati uporabnika " + username + "?");
            if (r == true) {
                $.get( "/jq/user_chat_actions.php?block&conversation_id=" + conversation_id, function( data ) {
                    $("#sender-conversation-" + conversation_id).remove();
                    $("#conversation-" + conversation_id).remove();
                });
            }
            return false;
        }

        function hide_conversation(conversation_id, username)
        {
            var r = confirm("Želite skriti pogovor z uporabnikom " + username + "?");
            if (r == true) {
                $.get( "/jq/user_chat_actions.php?hide&conversation_id=" + conversation_id, function( data ) {
                    $(".kontakt #sender-conversation-" + conversation_id).remove();
                    $(".kontakt #conversation-" + conversation_id).remove();
                    $("#inbox-" + conversation_id).addClass('hidden-message invisible');
                });
            }
            return false;
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            $(".s_click").on("click", function (e) {
                avoidNSError($(this).data('param'));
            });
        });

(function($){
	$.fn.extend({
		fixcenter: function () {
			return this.each(function() {
				var left = (  ( $(window).width() - $(this).outerWidth() ) / 2  );
				//alert($(window).width() + ' - ' + $(this).outerWidth() + ' : ' + left);
				$('#k17').append(' | ' + $(window).width() + ' - ' + $(this).outerWidth() + ' : ' + left);
				$(this).css({position:'fixed', left: (left < 0 ? left : 0)+'px'});
			});
		}
	});
})(jQuery);

$('#ad-bg div:first').fixcenter();
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#ad-bg div:first').fixcenter();
	$(window).resize(function(){
		$('#ad-bg div:first').fixcenter();
	});
});

        function save_ad(data_id){
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/jq/so.php",
                data: {id:data_id},
                async: true,
                cache: false,
                error: function(response)
                {
                    alert(response);
                },
                success: function(data){
                    if(data == 'true') {
                        //savethis.addClass('ikona-ok').delay(4000).hide('slow');
                        $("#save-ad-" + data_id).delay(150).fadeOut('slow');
                        $("#msave-ad-" + data_id).delay(150).fadeOut('slow');
                    } else {
                        alert(data);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

            $(".facet .more").mouseover(function() {
                $(this).addClass("open");
            });
            $(".facet .more").mouseleave(function() {
                if ( $(this).find('input[type=text]').is(":focus") ) {
                    if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry/i.test(navigator.userAgent) == false ) {
                        $(".facet .more").not(this).removeClass("open");

                }
            });

        function generate_filter_url(filter_url) {
            filter_url = filter_url.replace(/;/gmi, '');
            form_action = params_unserialize($('#sform').attr('action'));
            form_action = form_action.replace(/;/gmi, '');

            // console.log(filter_url);
            // console.log(form_action);

            filter_url = filter_url + '' + form_action;
            filter_url = filter_url.replace(/red=1/gmi, '');
            // console.log(filter_url);

            var wpg = $('body').attr('id');

            /*filter result count*/
            $.get( "/jq/count.php?wpg="+ wpg + "&" + filter_url, function( res ) {
                $("#ok").html(s_filter + ' [' + res + ']');
            });
            /*filter url*/
            $.post( "/jq/search.php?wpg="+ wpg + "&" + filter_url, function( res ) {
                $("#ok").attr('data-filter', res);
            });

        }

        function params_unserialize(p) {
            var ret = '',
                seg = p.replace(/^\?/,'').split(/&|\?/),
                len = seg.length, i = 1, s;
            for (;i<len;i++) {
                if (!seg[i]) { continue; }
                s = seg[i].split('=');
                ret += ';&'+s[0]+'='+s[1];
            }
            return ret;
        }


        $('.filter a.filter-icon').on('click', function () {
            $(".facet").dialog({
                modal: true,
                title: s_filter,
                cache: false,
                // autoOpen: false,
                buttons: [
                    {
                        id: "ok",
                        text: s_filter,
                        click: function() {
                            /*don't use .data it's cached*/
                            var filter_url = $('#ok').attr('data-filter');
                            window.location.href = filter_url;
                        }
                    },
                    {
                        id: "close",
                        text: s_cancle,
                        click: function() {
                            location.reload();
                        }
                    }
                ],
                close: function(event, ui) {
                    location.reload();
                },
                open: function () {
                    $(this).parent().promise().done(function () {

                        /*value of filed with thousand . seperator*/
                        if ($('#sform [name=c1]').val() != undefined) $('#sform [name=c1]').val($('#sform [name=c1]').val().replace(/\./gmi, ''));
                        if ($('#sform [name=c2]').val() != undefined) $('#sform [name=c2]').val($('#sform [name=c2]').val().replace(/\./gmi, ''));

                        if ($('#sform [name=z1]').val() != undefined)  $('#sform [name=z1]').val($('#sform [name=z1]').val().replace(/\./gmi, ''));
                        if ($('#sform [name=z2]').val() != undefined)  $('#sform [name=z2]').val($('#sform [name=z2]').val().replace(/\./gmi, ''));

                        var filter_url = decodeURI($('#sform').serialize());
                        var form_action = params_unserialize($('#sform').attr('action'));

                        filter_url = filter_url.replace(/&/gmi, ';&');
                        // console.log(filter_url + form_action);
                        generate_filter_url(filter_url + form_action);

                        /*filter item click*/
                        /*Vrsta posredovanja filter item click*/
                        $('.posredovanja .dropdownPanel a').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&p(.*?)[^;]*/igm;

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            $('.posredovanja .dropdownLabel').html($(this).text() + '<i class="fa fa-caret-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>');

                            var val = $(this).data('val');
                            if (val == undefined) {
                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                                return;
                            }

                            var param = '&p='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                            filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Država filter item click*/
                        $('.country .dropdownPanel a').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&d(.*?)[^;]*/igm;

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            $('.country .dropdownLabel').html($(this).text() + '<i class="fa fa-caret-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>');

                            /*If country is selected then show regions dropdown*/
                            var id = $(this).data('val');
                            if ($('.dropdownWrapper.regije').length)
                                $('.dropdownWrapper.regije').remove();

                            $.post("/jq/r-sel-mobile.php", {id:id,rsel:''}, function(data) {
                                $('.dropdownWrapper.country').after(data);
                            });

                            var param = '&d='+id+';';
                            filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            /*Reload new UE on Država change*/
                                /*Preselected Regija*/
                                var regex_r = /&r(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex_r, '');
                                if (id == 197) {
                                    var param_r = '&r=14;';
                                    var id_r = 14;
                                }
                                else if (id == 55){
                                    var param_r = '&r=33;';
                                    var id_r = 33;
                                }

                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param_r);

                                /*remove preselected UE and Naselja*/
                                $('#facetUE a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                    var param = '&ue[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                    filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                                });
                                $('#facetNaselja a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                    var param = '&naselja[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                    filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                                });

                                $('#facetUE').empty();
                                $('#facetNaselja').empty();

                                /*Load new UE*/
                                $.post("/jq/ue-sel.php", {id:id_r}, function(data) {
                                    $('#facetUE').append(data);
                                });


                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Regije filter item click*/
                        $('#sform').on('click', '.regije .dropdownPanel a', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&r(.*?)[^;]*/igm;

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            $('.regije .dropdownLabel').html($(this).text() + '<i class="fa fa-caret-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>');

                            var id = $(this).data('val');
                            if (id == undefined) {
                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                                return;
                            }

                            var param = '&r='+id+';';
                            filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            /*remove preselected UE and Naselja*/
                            $('#facetUE a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                var param = '&ue[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            });
                            $('#facetNaselja a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                var param = '&naselja[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            });

                            $('#facetUE').empty();
                            $('#facetNaselja').empty();

                            /*Load new UE*/
                            $.post("/jq/ue-sel-mobile.php", {id:id}, function(data) {
                                $('#facetUE').append(data);
                            });

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Ključne besede*/
                        $('.fsearch.keywords').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&q=(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            var q = $('#q').val();
                            var param = '&q=' + q +';';

                            if (q != undefined)
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Tip nepremičnine filter item click*/
                        $('.nepremicnine .dropdownPanel a').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&n(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                            var id = $(this).data('val');

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            $('.nepremicnine .dropdownLabel').html($(this).text() + '<i class="fa fa-caret-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>');

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);

                            /*Reload new Tipi on Tip nepremičnine change*/
                                /*remove preselected Tipi*/
                                $('#facetTipi a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                    var param = '&t[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                    filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                                    generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                                });

                                /*show new Tipi*/
                                $('#facetTipi').empty();
                                $.post("/jq/t-sel-mobile.php", {id:id}, function(data) {
                                    $('#facetTipi').append(data);
                                });

                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Tipi nepremičnin*/
                        $('#sform').on('click', '#facetTipi a:not(.icon)', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();

                            var param = '&t[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                            if ($(this).hasClass('act')) {
                                $(this).removeClass('act');
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            }
                            else {
                                $(this).addClass('act actMob');
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);
                            }

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Nadstropje filter item click*/
                        $('.nadstropje .dropdownPanel a').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&nadst(.*?)[^;]*/igm;

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                        /*Nadstropje filter from/to item click*/
                        $('.nadst .fsearch').on('click', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var regex = /&nadst(.*?)[^;]*;/igm;

                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                            var param = '&nadst[]='+$('#nadst_od').val()+';&nadst[]='+$('#nadst_do').val()+';';

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Upravne enote*/
                        $('#sform').on('click', '#facetUE a:not(.icon)', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var id = $(this).data('val');

                            var param = '&ue[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                            if ($(this).hasClass('act')) {
                                $(this).removeClass('act');
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            }
                            else {
                                $(this).addClass('act actMob');
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);
                            }

                            /* refresh Naselja on UE change */
                            var ue = $('#facetUE a.act').length;
                            if (ue == 1) {

                                if (!$('#facetNaselja').length) {
                                    $('#facetUE').parent().after('<h3 class="naselja_t">Naselja</h3><fieldset class="radio-group"><ul id="facetNaselja"></ul></fieldset>');
                                }

                                $('#facetNaselja').empty();

                                $.post("/jq/n-sel-mobile.php", {id:$('#facetUE a.act').data('val')}, function(data) {
                                    $('#facetNaselja').append(data);
                                    $('.naselja_t').show();
                                    $('#facetNaselja').parent().show();
                                });
                            }
                            else {
                                $('#facetNaselja a.act').each(function( index ) {
                                    var param = '&naselja[]='+$(this).data('val')+';';
                                    filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                                });
                                $('.naselja_t').hide();
                                $('#facetNaselja').parent().hide();
                                $('#facetNaselja').empty();
                            }

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Upravne enote*/
                        $('#sform').on('click', '#facetNaselja a:not(.icon)', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();

                        /*Add generate url for Cena*/

                            e.preventDefault();

                            $('#facetCena a:not(.icon)').not(this).removeClass('act');

                                var s2 = res[1].split('-');

                                var param = '&' + s1[0] + '=' + s1[1] + '&' + s2[0] + '=' + s2[1]+';';

                            }
                        });
                            /*Add generate url for custom Cena*/
                            $('.more.cena input[type=submit]').on('click', function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                var regex = /&c1=(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                                var val_from = $('.more.cena input[name=c1]').val();
                                if (val_from == undefined)
                                    val_from = '*';
                                var val_to = $('.more.cena input[name=c2]').val();
                                if (val_to == undefined)
                                    val_to = '*';

                                if ($('.more.cena .cm2').val() == 1)
                                    var param = '&c1=' + val_from.replace(/\./gmi, '') + '&c2=' + val_to.replace(/\./gmi, '') + '&cm2=1' + ';';
                                else
                                    var param = '&c1=' + val_from.replace(/\./gmi, '') + '&c2=' + val_to.replace(/\./gmi, '') +';';


                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                            });
                            /*remove custom setted velikost */
                            $('.ui-dialog .ui-dialog-content .nadst .icon.clr.ur').on('click', function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                var regex = /&nadst(.*?)[^;]*;/igm;
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                                var param = '&nadst[]=vsa;&nadst[]=vsa;';
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                                $("#nadst_od")[0].selectedIndex = 0;
                                $("#nadst_do")[0].selectedIndex = 0;

                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                            });
                            /*remove custom setted velikost */
                            $('.ui-dialog .ui-dialog-content #facetCena .icon.clr.ur').on('click', function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();

                                var regex = /&c1=(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');
                                var regex = /&c2=(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');

                                var default_vals = JSON.parse('["{\\"text\\":\\"do - 500\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-0;c2-500\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"500 - 1000\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-500;c2-1000\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"1000 - 1500\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-1000;c2-1500\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"1500 - 2000\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-1500;c2-2000\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"2000 - 2500\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-2000;c2-2500\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"2500 - 3000\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-2500;c2-3000\\"}","{\\"text\\":\\"3000 in ve\\u010d\\",\\"val\\":\\"c1-3000;c2-*\\"}"]');
                                $('#facetCena').empty();
                                for (var i = 0, len = default_vals.length; i < len; ++i) {
                                    var size = JSON.parse(default_vals[i]);
                                    $('#facetCena').append('<li><a href="#" data-val="'+size.val+'">'+size.text+'</a></li>');
                                }

                                $("input[name='c1']").val('');
                                $("input[name='c2']").val('');

                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                            });

                        /*Add generate url for Datum vpisa*/
                        $('#last').on('change', function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();

                            var val = $(this).val();
                            if (val == undefined) {
                                generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                                return;
                            }

                            var param = '&last='+val+';';
                            filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Vsi oglasi*/
                        $('#f0').on('click', function(e) {
                            var param = '&f=;';
                            if($(this).is(":checked")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);
                            }
                            else if($(this).is(":not(:checked)")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            }
                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Znižana cena*/
                        $('#f1').on('click', function(e) {
                            var param = '&f=1;';
                            if($(this).is(":checked")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);
                            }
                            else if($(this).is(":not(:checked)")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            }
                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Zasebna ponudba*/
                        $('#f2').on('click', function(e) {
                            var param = '&f=2;';
                            if($(this).is(":checked")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);
                            }
                            else if($(this).is(":not(:checked)")){
                                filter_url = filter_url.replace(param, '');
                            }
                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });

                        /*Add generate url for Studenti*/
                        $('#student').on('click', function(e) {
                            var regex = /&student(.*?)[^;]*/igm;
                            filter_url = filter_url.replace(regex, '');


                            var param = '&student=1;';
                            if($(this).is(":checked"))
                                filter_url = filter_url.concat(param);

                            generate_filter_url(filter_url);
                        });
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

            </div><!-- /980 -->
